<td style=" text-align: center;margin:auto; vertical-align:top"><ix:nonNumeric contextRef="duration_2023-12-07_to_2023-12-07_us-gaap-StatementClassOfStockAxis_msft-NotesTwoPointSixTwoFivePercentDueMayTwoTwentyThirtyThreeMember" name="dei:SecurityExchangeName">NASDAQ</ix:nonNumeric></td></tr> </table><p style="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Indicate by check mark whether the registrant is an emerging growth company as defined in Rule 405 of the Securities Act of 1933 (&#167;230.405 of this chapter) or Rule 12b-2 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 (&#167;240.12b-2 of this chapter).</p><p style="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Emerging growth company <ix:nonNumeric contextRef="duration_2023-12-07_to_2023-12-07" name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" format="ixt-sec:boolballotbox">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></p><p style="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has Re-elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act. &#9744;</p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p><p style="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p><p style="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p></div></div><p style='page-break-before:always'></p> <hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" /> <div style="text-align:center"> <div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto"><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;5.07. Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders</p><p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On December&#160;7, 2022, Microsoft Corporation (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) held its 2023 Annual Shareholders Meeting (the &#8220;Annual Meeting&#8221;). There were 7,429,030,596 shares of common stock entitled to be voted at the Annual Meeting, of which 6,340,975,646 were voted in person or by proxy. The results for each item submitted for a vote of shareholders are as follows. The shareholders:</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(1) Voted to elect each of the twelve (12)&#160;nominees for director.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(2) Approved, on an advisory basis, the compensation of the Company&#8217;s named executive officers.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(3) Approved, on an advisory basis, a frequency of every year for the Company&#8217;s advisory vote to approve the compensation of the Company&#8217;s named executive officers. Consistent with the recommendation of the Directors and the majority of votes cast, the Company has determined that future advisory votes to approve the compensation of the Company&#8217;s named executive officers will take place every year until the next advisory vote on the frequency of such votes, which will occur no later than the Company&#8217;s Annual Shareholders Meeting in 2029.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(4) Voted to ratify the appointment of Deloitte&#160;&amp; Touche LLP as the Company&#8217;s independent registered public accounting firm for fiscal year 2024.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(5) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on gender-based compensation and benefits gaps.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(6) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on risk from omitting ideology in EEO Policy.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(7) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on government takedown requests.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(8) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on<span style="font-weight:bold">&#160;</span>risks of weapons development.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(9) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on climate risks to retirement plan beneficiaries.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(10) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on tax transparency.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(11) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on data operations in human rights hotspots.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(12) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a mandate for third-party political reporting.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(13) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on artificial intelligence misinformation and disinformation.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company&#8217;s inspector of election certified the following vote tabulations:</p><p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Election of Directors</p><p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
